\nlocal MAIN_SCREENGUI = nil\nlocal function detectMainGui()\n    for _, scr in ipairs(CoreGui:GetChildren()) do\n        if scr:IsA('ScreenGui') then\n            for _, d in ipairs(scr:GetDescendants()) do\n                if (d:IsA('TextLabel') or d:IsA('TextButton')) then\n                    local txt = tostring(d.Text or ''):lower()\n                    if txt:match('farming') or txt:match('robbing') or txt:match('teleport') or txt:match('haki') or txt:match('weapon') then\n                        MAIN_SCREENGUI = scr\n                        return scr\n                    end\n                end\n            end\n        end\n    end\n    return nil\nend
\nlocal function flameToggleAction()\n    if not MAIN_SCREENGUI then\n        notify.Show('Menu not loaded yet (press HIEN VIP)', 1.8)\n        return\n    end\n    pcall(function()\n        MAIN_SCREENGUI.Enabled = not MAIN_SCREENGUI.Enabled\n        notify.Show(MAIN_SCREENGUI.Enabled and 'Menu shown' or 'Menu hidden', 1.2)\n    end)\nend

\nlocal function load_original_code()\n    if _G._HIENVIP_ORIG_LOADED then\n        notify.Show('Full menu already loaded',1.4)\n        return\n    end\n    FastOptimize()\n    notify.Show('ðŸ”¥ HIEN LOADING FULL MENU ðŸ”¥', 2.8)\n    task.wait(0.06)\n    local ok, chunk = pcall(function()\n        -- try HttpService Base64 decode if available\n        local ok2, hs = pcall(function() return game:GetService('HttpService') end)\n        if ok2 and hs and hs.Base64Decode then\n            return hs:Base64Decode(orig_b64)\n        end\n        return nil\n    end)\n    local chunk_text = nil\n    if ok and chunk then chunk_text = chunk else\n        -- fallback manual decode\n        local b='ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/'\n        local data = orig_b64:gsub('[^'..b..'=]', '')\n        local s = data:gsub('.', function(x)\n            if x == '=' then return '' end\n            local r,f = '', (b:find(x)-1)\n            for i=6,1,-1 do r = r .. (f%2^i - f%2^(i-1) > 0 and '1' or '0') end\n            return r\n        end)\n        local out = s:gsub('%d%d%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?%d?', function(x)\n            if #x ~= 8 then return '' end\n            local c = 0\n            for i=1,8 do c = c + (x:sub(i,i) == '1' and 2^(8-i) or 0) end\n            return string.char(c)\n        end)\n        chunk_text = out\n    end\n    if not chunk_text then notify.Show('Failed to decode original', 3); return end\n    local ok2, err = pcall(function()\n        local f = loadstring(chunk_text)\n        if not f then error('loadstring failed') end\n        f()\n    end)\n    if not ok2 then notify.Show('Error loading menu: '..tostring(err), 4)\n    else\n        _G._HIENVIP_ORIG_LOADED = true\n        task.delay(0.12, function() detectMainGui(); -- attempt hide about/gems remnants\n            pcall(function() for _, scr in ipairs(CoreGui:GetChildren()) do for _, d in ipairs(scr:GetDescendants()) do\n                if (d:IsA('TextLabel') or d:IsA('TextButton')) then local txt = tostring(d.Text or ''):lower() if txt:find('about') or txt:find('gems') or txt:find('risky') then if d.Parent and d.Parent:IsA('GuiObject') then d.Parent.Visible = false end end end end end end)\n            notify.Show('HIEN VIP â€” MENU LOADED', 2)\n        end)\n    end\nend
\nlauncher.Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() load_original_code() end)
\ndo local last=0; launcher.Button.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function() local now=tick(); if now-last<0.35 then launcher.Gui.Enabled = not launcher.Gui.Enabled end; last=now end) end
